for
Song
of
the
Year">Song
of
the
Year</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Record_of_the_Year?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Record
of
the
Year"
class="mw-redirect">Record
of
the
Year</a>,
for
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Just_the_Way_You_Are_(Billy_Joel_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Just
the
Way
You
Are
(Billy
Joel
song)">Just
the
Way
You
Are</a>&quot;.</p>








<p>He
was
inducted
into
the
<a
href="/wiki/Long_Island_Music_Hall_of_Fame?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Long
Island
Music
Hall
of
Fame">Long
Island
Music
Hall
of
Fame</a>
on
October
15,
2006.
In
2005,
Joel
received
a
star
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/Hollywood_Walk_of_Fame?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hollywood
Walk
of
Fame">Hollywood
Walk
of
Fame</a>.</p>








<p>Joel
is
the
only
performing
artist
to
have
played
both
<a
href="/wiki/Yankee_Stadium_(1923)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Yankee
Stadium
(1923)">Yankee</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Shea_Stadium?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Shea
Stadium">Shea
Stadiums</a>,
as
well
as
<a
href="/wiki/Giants_Stadium?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Giants
Stadium">Giants
Stadium</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Madison_Square_Garden?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Madison
Square
Garden">Madison
Square
Garden</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Nassau_Veterans_Memorial_Coliseum?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nassau
Veterans
Memorial
Coliseum">Nassau
Veterans
Memorial
Coliseum</a>.
Joel
has
banners
in
the
rafters
of
the
<a
href="/wiki/Times_Union_Center?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Times
Union
Center">Times
Union
Center</a>,
Nassau
Coliseum,
Madison
Square
Garden,
<a
href="/wiki/Mohegan_Sun_Arena?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mohegan
Sun
Arena">Mohegan
Sun
Arena</a>
in
Uncasville,
Connecticut,
<a
href="/wiki/Wells_Fargo_Center_(Philadelphia)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Wells
Fargo
Center
(Philadelphia)">Wells
Fargo
Center</a>
in
Philadelphia,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Hartford_Civic_Center?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hartford
Civic
Center"
class="mw-redirect">Hartford
Civic
Center</a>
in
Hartford.
(Joel
is
erroneously
cited
as
the
first
artist
to
perform
a
concert
at
Yankee
Stadium
in
New
York
City;
<a
href="/wiki/The_Isley_Brothers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Isley
Brothers">The
Isley
Brothers</a>
first
performed
there
in
1969,
and
the
Latin
supergroup
The
<a
href="/wiki/Fania_All-Stars?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Fania
All-Stars">Fania
All-Stars</a>
played
and
recorded
live
albums
at
the
stadium
during
the
1970s.)</p>








<p>He
has
also
sponsored
the
Billy
Joel
Visiting
Composer
Series
at
<a
href="/wiki/Syracuse_University?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Syracuse
University">Syracuse
University</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-77"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-77"><span>[</span>77<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>On
December
12,
2011
Joel
became
the
first
non-classical
musician
honored
with
a
portrait
in
<a
href="/wiki/Steinway?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Steinway"
class="mw-redirect">Steinway
Hall</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-78"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-78"><span>[</span>78<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
December
2013
in
Washington,
D.C.,
Joel
received
<a
href="/wiki/Kennedy_Center_Honors?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kennedy
Center
Honors">Kennedy
Center
Honors</a>,
the
nation's
highest
honor
for
influencing
American
culture
through
the
arts.<sup
id="cite_ref-Billboard20131208_79-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Billboard20131208-79"><span>[</span>79<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

Award</a>
Show,
Joel
extended
his

of
&quot;The
River
of
Dreams&quot;
by
stopping
the
song
partway
through,
looking
at

with

while
pretending
to
check
his

and
saying,
&quot;valuable
advertising
time
going
by...dollars...dollars...dollars...&quot;
which
was
met
with
laughter
from
the
audience.
He
then
resumed
playing
the
song.
This
was
done
in
response
to
<a
href="/wiki/Frank_Sinatra?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"

Sinatra">Frank
Sinatra</a>

cut
off
on
television
while
giving
an
acceptance
speech
when
given
a
lifetime
achievement
Grammy.</li>

(musical)">Movin'

(2002),

<a

theater"

on
December

Joel
was

Orchestrations">Tony
Award
for
Best
Orchestrations</a>.

musical
is
really
a
dance
performance
choreographed
by
famed

<a

Joel's

sung
by
<a

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Billy_Joel&page=1&ac=24&qid=4A10C963DA0045166D9D4D3DE503023C&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>
